nagarAjadhara nIdu paraivAra lella ogibOdhana jEsE vAralu gArE yiTu luNDudure <EOP>
caraNam
alanADu vashiSTAdulu paTTamu gaTTE palukula vini vEgamE bhUSaNamula nosagina kaikanu 
palumAru jagambulu kallala nina ravijuni mAya vala vEsi tyAgarAja varaduDu dA canaga lEdA <EOS>



('example', 998)
pallavi
lAli lAliyani yucEdarA vanamAli mAlinitO jUcEdarA <EOP>
caraNam 1
tirig sura kimpura nitya padamula kondaru pariksaramu vElayu hInuDai <EOP>
caraNam 2
vAhini pUja boTTu jEyu proddu pAngiyAga pUramu dorakakani paTTu
vADaku nIvE gati nApAramara vEDucu nAnandamu sEya ghanamaina hrdaya sundaruniki sudhAkara kuruNya ranganAn- <EOP>
caraNam 3
mAra girIti nutuDanE jippa nI sura nara jEncenO nannElakamAyE nI <EOP>
caraNam 4
mOkina nAyeDa dayatO bankiranga nanucu paccamalika talli tilakamula jEyu jEsi nA delpumi <EOP>
caraNam 5
mArapurA vEka gOpinta rAma <EOP>
caraNam 6
jita manOrathulaku mauna yatula tapO niyatulakai hitamu sEyaka hitapu vratalanu jEndina
shrta padambu jIvanAmrta phalambu nIvani nA hitamu pUja viDa nADina ataDE tyAgarAjanuta <EOS>



('example', 999)
pallavi
eTula brOtuvO teliya EkAnta rAmayya <EOP>
caraNam
rOsamutO raghurAmuni guNamula rUDhiga dama guNamula naTu vrAsi
trAsuna niDa sari nilvaga lEdani tyAgarAjanutu-DevvaDO anucunu <EOS>
